After Abdication, the Wise King of Siam Refuses to Talk About Politics 30

Ten Conditions Rejected by Parliament

Reforming the Constitution, the Ambition is Contrary to the Wish

Cranleigh, England - After abdicating, the King of Siam, using the title of Prince Sukhothai, recently gave an interview to the press, remaining silent on political matters and showing no signs of worry or sorrow, only saying that he and his wife were very happy to live in Britain. He then told reporters in a humorous tone that reporters from various countries had previously misunderstood the Siamese court etiquette and used "Brother of the Moon" as the king's honorific title, and they should not do so in the future.

Ten Conditions

According to reports, there are ten conditions for the King of Siam to be reinstated, as follows: (1) Half of the members of parliament are not elected by the people. According to the constitution, the government appoints them. In the future, they should be jointly selected by civil servants and the government. (2) Naval and army officers should not attend parliament or interfere in politics in the future. (3) Regarding the king's veto power, previously only a majority decision of parliament was required to override it. In the future, it should be decided by a three-quarters majority of parliament or by a popular vote. (4) The people should have the freedom of assembly and association and to publish opinions or give speeches and propaganda in newspapers. (5) Constitutional guarantees should be included in the criminal law, and all political lawsuits should be tried by ordinary courts. (6) All political prisoners should be granted amnesty. (7) All civil servants who have been dismissed due to political relations should be reinstated. (8) Crimes against the constitution should not be investigated. (9) Troops should be stationed at the Royal Palace permanently. (10) No death sentence should be carried out before the king has decided whether to grant a pardon. The above conditions were rejected by the Siamese Parliament, so the king decided to abdicate. (3rd Havas Telegram)

Concern for the People's Suffering

[London] As a result of his abdication, the King of Siam will henceforth be known as Prince Sakdaya. In his abdication edict, the King of Siam criticized the tyrannical behavior of the Siamese government. The King of Siam said that he was willing to give his privileges to the people, but he was unwilling to give them to any individual or political party, as the purpose of these people was nothing more than to abuse their privileges for personal gain. Finally, the King of Siam said, "I am now unable to serve my motherland and my people any longer. I am deeply sorry, but I only hope that the Siamese people can be happy." (4th National Telegram)

Young Nephew Succeeds

Noel Park, England - The secretary of the King of Siam announced today that the King of Siam has formally abdicated. The abdication edict was signed at 1:45 p.m. on Saturday and immediately sent to the Siamese Embassy in London. The secretary also said that the King of Siam's eleven-year-old nephew, Prince Ananda, may inherit the throne. As for the reasons for the King of Siam's abdication, the secretary said that it was because the Siamese cabinet led by Colonel Bahol had completely rejected the King of Siam's demands for government reform. Now the King of Siam will temporarily reside in London until after June, and then the plans have not been decided, and will depend entirely on the environment. (3rd National Telegram)

Pessimistic About the Political Situation

[London] The Times stated in an editorial today that the Siamese political situation is very unstable and the country's future is very uncertain. This situation is becoming increasingly clear due to three factors: (1) the explanation of the King of Siam's abdication, (2) the points of contention between the King of Siam and the Siamese government, and the government's maintenance of the 1933 legislation to deal with the military revolution. Left-wing politicians hope to cross the gap between hereditary aristocracy and constitutional monarchy in one fell swoop, but their actions have now failed. Their sudden mobilization has led to the future responsibility of Congress, the government, and the royal family, and it is feared that their future will be detrimental to both the government and the royal family. (4th Reuters Telegram)

The Pound Falls, the United States Considers Countermeasures 31

Likely to Use Funds for Relief

The International Currency War Intensifies

[Washington] Today's news is that government officials are paying close attention to the soaring gold prices in London, which are setting new records every day. At the same time, they are also paying attention to the falling pound, which has reached its lowest price in the New York exchange market since October 1933. They are completely silent on the current international monetary situation, but it is generally believed that they are already discussing plans to deal with the falling pound, as the falling pound may have a deflationary impact on US prices, which would conflict with President Roosevelt's plan. Now the pound has fallen to an extent that exceeds the fall of the dollar, so that the dollar is at its highest level in years compared to the pound. The Treasury Department is still not surprised on the surface, but claims that the government has not yet used the $200 million stabilization fund and can provide relief when necessary. They are unwilling to criticize the saying that the United States will further reduce the value of the dollar to offset the benefits of the falling pound. According to news from Paris, the French authorities believe that the current situation in London is very dangerous, and they are very afraid that after the pound falls further, the British stabilization fund will not be able to stop it. If so, the European gold countries will have no choice but to devalue their currencies. As for Treasury Secretary Morgenthau, he does not yet believe that the situation is so serious that it is necessary to use the stabilization fund. (3rd National Telegram)

[Tokyo] In the international exchange market, the pound has continued to fall for days, and on the morning of the 4th, it broke through the 28-yen barrier and fell to 27.87 yen. According to the Deputy Governor of the Bank of Japan, Fukai, there are various theories about the reasons for the fall in the British pound, but the instability of the political situation in Britain is the primary reason. In addition, the British current year's international balance of payments showed that expenditures exceeded 1 million pounds. British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain stated in Parliament that Britain has no intention of stabilizing the exchange rate by agreement. For these reasons, short-term foreign capital entering Britain from foreign countries has continued to flow out of the country. If Britain uses a huge amount of funds for this, the pound may fall even further. (4th Japan United Press Telegram)

[New York] A Wall Street financial authority stated today that the decline in the pound may be a turning point in global currency stability. His theory is that if the fall in the pound forces France to abandon the gold standard, then the United States and Britain will quickly seek ways to prevent the franc from falling too much. A sharp fall in the franc will trigger a global currency war, and as a result, all countries involved will be harmed. Therefore, all countries will try their best to avoid this. The authority continued, "If France and other gold standard countries are forced to abandon the gold standard, then other countries will be forced to agree to stabilize the franc. This is truly a turning point for recovery." (3rd National Telegram)

Franc Devaluation Possible

[Paris] The French financial community believes that it is possible for the French franc to reduce its gold value. According to reliable sources, the technical division of the French Ministry of Finance was recently ordered to study in detail the position of the Bank of France, the national financial system, and the national debt management methods after various degrees of currency devaluation. It is reported that the technical division has completed the study of various situations under the degrees of 5%, 10%, 15%, 20%, 25%, and 30% devaluation, so the authorities can now understand the general situation after suddenly reducing the gold value of the franc. (4th Reuters Telegram)

Beijing - Official circles claim that although the value of the British pound has fallen, it will not force Belgium to devalue its currency. (4th National Telegram)

The Greek Government is Confident it Can Control the Situation 34

Using the Air Force to Survey and Suppress the Rebellion

Athens - The Greek government has refused to accept any compromise with the rebels and is striving to conquer the revolution. Government troops in the Drama area have defeated the rebels and then advanced to occupy the town of Kavala, so all of Macedonia and western Serres are now under government control. Yesterday, the government and rebels clashed in eastern Crete, and they are still fighting each other. The result is still unclear. Although Crete is the hometown of Venizelos, who has served as the Greek Prime Minister eight times and supports this revolution, it is reported that many civilians there have also joined the government to fight the rebels. Yesterday, the cabinet held a special meeting and decided to refuse any compromise with the rebels. The cabinet has obtained the President's approval and ordered Army Chief General Kondylis, together with Generals Mantaitzis and Dousmanis, to take any military measures and fully deal with this rebellion. Kondylis immediately led the troops in Macedonia and northern Greece and began attacking this morning, resulting in the occupation of Drama and Kavala. Since Kondylis had to go north to command, the affairs of the Ministry of the Army were temporarily taken over by General Mantaitzis. The government made considerable use of aircraft in this campaign. All civilian aircraft were requisitioned by the government yesterday for deployment. Some aircraft continued to bomb the Avroloff cruiser and the rebel ships in Suda Bay yesterday afternoon. At the same time, Venizelos's residence in Chania was bombed by the air force, causing many casualties. The rebel ships also fired artillery at the aircraft in return, but it is reported that there were no casualties on the government side. Venizelos's Liberal Party split yesterday, and the majority faction sent a telegram to Venizelos, saying that the revolutionary action was doomed to failure and would be irreversible if it did not stop immediately. (National Telegram, 4th)

The five ships are currently moored in Suda Bay, Crete, from which Venizelos's residence can be seen. Government aircraft were only ordered to drop bombs around the ships to avoid damaging them. One theory is that during the aircraft attack, one of the ships suddenly emitted thick smoke, which must have been caused by a direct hit causing serious damage. (Reuters, 3rd)

It is now known that when government artillery units bombarded Perama yesterday morning, they severely damaged the destroyers Niki and Leon, as well as a submarine. It is expected that if the ships do not surrender immediately, government forces will launch a real bombardment. The result is still unknown. The government has now begun mobilization and sent troops to the province of Macedonia. The process is going smoothly, and a large number of people have volunteered to join the volunteer team. He will never accept a position to work with Venizelos. (Reuters, 3rd)

I love Venizelos very much, but he is a politician and I am a soldier, so our political views are different." He also said that if he (Plastiras) were to go to Greece now, he would be assassinated. However, if the majority of the people wanted him to take office, he would have no choice but to do so. (Havas News Agency, 3rd)

Hungarian Political Tide 36

Only Three Former Members Continue to Serve

Although the parliament has not been in session, the political struggle has been going on for a long time in private conversations, public gatherings, and newspaper commentaries. Legislative Yuan's Criminal Committee Organizes Special Criminal Laws and Regulations 40

[Nanjing] - The Criminal Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan has held eight meetings and has completed the review of the draft implementation regulations for the Criminal Law and Criminal Procedure Law. After the Criminal Law is promulgated and implemented, the Criminal Committee, in accordance with the instructions of the Central Government, has added to the organization of special criminal laws and regulations. Those proposed to be abolished include the Emergency Law for Punishing Acts Endangering the Republic of China, the Provisional Regulations for Punishing Bandits, and the Opium Suppression Law and its implementation rules. Those proposed to be amended include the Communist Self-Surrender Law, etc. Those proposed to be retained include the Military Secrets Protection Law, etc. The Criminal Committee will submit the case of organizing special criminal laws and regulations to Director Sun, suggesting that the Central Committee examine and decide on it. Ministry of Railways Urges Expedited Procurement Procedures 68

[Nanjing] The Ministry of Railways reports that the procedures for material procurement, customs declaration, delivery, inspection, and reporting from various railways often take more than a month, or even two to three months. According to the Ministry's precedent, payment for material procurement contracts, unless otherwise specified, is generally settled within three weeks after delivery and acceptance. Suppliers often urge payment upon maturity, but because the inspection report has not yet reached the Ministry, it is impossible to verify, resulting in delays. This situation violates the contract and affects credibility. Therefore, all railway bureaus are ordered that once materials arrive, they must immediately declare customs and take delivery to expedite inspection. The Ministry's inspection fees should be inspected and reported within three weeks after each batch of materials is delivered. (4th Special Dispatch)

Tianjin Drug Rehabilitation Center Opens Yesterday 80

[Tianjin] The Tianjin Drug Rehabilitation Center opened at 2:00 PM on the 4th, welcoming people from all walks of life to visit. A total of more than 500 people arrived. The center currently houses 291 drug addicts, of whom 107 have fully recovered their health and are scheduled to be released on the 6th. Currently, about 30 people apply for rehabilitation every day, and adult offenders account for 60-70% of them. In the first week after admission, emphasis is placed on drug treatment, and in the following two weeks, physical exercise and spiritual cultivation are carried out. After drug addiction is eliminated, new offenders have tattoos on their left arms, and repeat offenders are executed. According to Director Zhang Ting'e, the entire center can accommodate 500 people and is expected to expand to accommodate 1,000 people. A ward for female offenders is also under planning and can be realized in the short term. It takes more than 20 days for each drug addict to completely quit the habit, and the cost of food, clothing, and medicine is 20 yuan in total. It is reported that after entering the center, drug addicts gradually gain weight, with the fastest gaining up to 21 pounds. (4th Central News Agency Telegram)

Concrete Measures Agreed Upon for Mongolian Taxation Issue 94

Mongolian and Suiyuan Representatives Will Return to Report Separately

Beiping Correspondence: The Mongolian taxation issue is being actively mediated by the relevant parties in Beiping, Suiyuan, and Bailingmiao. Since the issue was essentially a misunderstanding between the two sides, the Mongolian Political Council's attitude immediately turned to one of reconciliation once it was explained. The Suiyuan Provincial Government also expressed its willingness to compromise. According to a telegram from Prince De to his representative Bao Yueqing, the resolution principle was discussed and decided with Xiao Renyuan and Chen Qin in Bailingmiao: (1) Wang Jingguo's troops stationed in Mongolian territory and the tax checkpoints they set up will be completely removed. (2) The boundaries of local taxes in Mongolia and Suiyuan should be clarified. (3) In the future, camels transporting goods through Mongolian territory will pay a transit tax of eight cents per head. After Xiao and Chen discussed and obtained the principles, they returned to Suiyuan at the end of last month to report to Fu Zuoyi. Fu considered it satisfactory, but the specific measures for implementation need to be agreed upon urgently. Therefore, Xiao and Chen left Suiyuan again yesterday (1st) for Bailingmiao to continue negotiations. According to relevant parties in Beiping, the specific measures for implementation are nothing more than Wang Jingguo's troops immediately withdrawing from the Mongolian region, and the Mongolian Political Council collecting local taxes in accordance with the principles of Mongolian autonomy for construction purposes. The collection of this transit tax does not constitute an excessive action within the scope of Mongolian autonomy, but the Mongolian Political Council will submit it to the Central Government for record before implementing the tax. Bao Yueqing, Prince De's representative in Beiping, visited He Yingqin at Jurentang at 11:00 AM this morning (2nd) and is scheduled to return to Bailingmiao to report on the mandate after tomorrow (3rd) (4th). Shi Huayan, the representative of the Suiyuan Provincial Government who stayed in Beiping to negotiate, will also return to Suiyuan in the coming days. (2nd)

Songjiang 95

Difficulties and Disturbances Caused by Refugees Passing Through Qingpu

The Zhejiang Refugee Reception Center established by the Songjiang Red Cross branch has taken in more than 3,000 refugees, both men and women, old and young, from Zhejiang Province. Suddenly, on the morning of the 4th, more than 200 refugees formed a team and entered the city. They went to the Daoxiangcun teashop east of the Public Security Bureau and grabbed anything they could eat. For a time, the goods displayed on the counter were emptied. Liang Jinrong, a resident of Wangdian, was arrested by the store. According to his confession, he came from Qingpu, and the reception center here could not accommodate them, so they entered the city to ask the Public Security Bureau for relief. The Public Security Bureau dispatched police to suppress the remaining refugees and escorted them out of the hospital.

Escaped Prisoner from Jail

A bandit prisoner named Lu Ajin, detained in the county jail, was originally sentenced to ten years. He had his sentence reduced by one-third due to the amnesty, leaving more than two years of his sentence. The prisoner was well-behaved in prison and was guaranteed by the Zhongxing Western Clothing Store on Puzhao Temple Street. He was assigned to outside duties and often went out to shop. He took it for granted. Unexpectedly, one day, he used the excuse of shopping and never returned. He disappeared without a trace, apparently escaping. The warden has investigated the case and ordered the Zhongxing Western Clothing Store to hand him over.

Suzhou 96

The Robbery Case at the Wenjia'an in the East of the City

At around 6:00 PM on the afternoon of the 3rd, seven robbers dressed in tattered uniforms and armed with weapons suddenly broke into the You Yangyu Inn at No. 40 Wenjia'an, Lindun Road. The owner of the inn is You Pinzhi. They first drove the five or six men and women of the family into the inner room and tied them up together. Then they proceeded to search and plunder. After about two hours, they searched and fled. After the robbers left, the family checked and found that they had been robbed of about a thousand gold worth of cash, jewelry, and clothing. They immediately reported to the police district and urged them to strictly arrest the robbers. After receiving the report, Zhang Hanwei, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, personally went to investigate and dispatched a large number of detectives to hunt down the robbers overnight. At that time, in order to facilitate the capture of the robbers, the city gate was closed for a time and then reopened. Suspicious pedestrians were checked. That night, the first branch arrested a suspect named Gao Degen at Qimen. Strict Director Yan of the First Branch offered a reward of 50 yuan for information leading to the arrest.

Wuxi 97

Extension Granted for Business Tax Payment Date

The local Business Tax Bureau was ordered to change the tax payment date, advancing it to the end of the second month of each quarter. Various businesses sent letters to the Chamber of Commerce, which forwarded them to the Finance Department, requesting an extension to the end of the last month. After receiving the presentation, Zhao, the Director of Finance, has already understood that the payment of business tax is allowed to be extended to the end of the quarter. If the tax can be paid within the time limit, no penalty will be added. If the tax is overdue, a late payment penalty of 10% will be added from the first day of the following month. A late payment penalty of 20% will be added from the 11th day. Those who fail to pay within one month will have their business suspended, and the county government will escort the payment of arrears and late payment penalties.

A Notorious Drug Pill Trafficker Arrested

Shen Qingcheng (from Changjing, Jiangyin), the assistant manager of the Licheng Steamship Company under the Gongyun Bridge and the manager of the Suqian Huaibei Dongji Steamship Company, is a notorious drug pill trafficker who has made a lot of profit. After the drug pill organization in Xiaoqingyang, Jiangyin, was cracked down by the county government last year, Shen escaped and remained at large. Recently, the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters received a secret report stating that Shen Qingcheng is now hiding in Wuxi and requested immediate arrest. After receiving the report, the headquarters secretly ordered the local County Public Security Bureau to investigate and arrest him. After receiving the order, Director Chen dispatched Inspector Ge Xinde, Wang Jixiong, and others to arrest Shen at No. 7 Xinliangxi Road. They also found a large number of letters and brought them to the bureau for temporary custody. He was transferred to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for interrogation yesterday.

Local News

Director Wu of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Reports on the Causes and Consequences of Public Panic in the City 99

Yesterday Morning at the Municipal Government's Expanded Memorial Week

According to the Central News Agency, the Municipal Government held an expanded memorial week yesterday morning, led by Mayor Wu, who presided over the ceremony. Director Wu Xingya of the Social Affairs Bureau gave a speech, which is recorded below:

Starting with the Shenxin No. 7 Factory Incident

Since then, the Shanghai market has been sluggish, and all industries have been declining. Although the closing accounts for the 23rd year were barely completed peacefully amidst the successive bank and money exchange closures and store bankruptcies, the difficulties and precarious situation of the industrial and commercial sectors remain very serious. At this time, the industrial and commercial sectors were requesting the central and local governments and the financial community to provide loans to rescue the market. Suddenly, the Shenxin No. 7 Factory was auctioned off by its first creditor, HSBC, because its overdue loan could not be repaid. Since the textile industry is a newly emerging national industry in our country, and Shenxin is a giant in this industry, the auctioned No. 7 Factory has more than 56,000 spindles, more than 7,100 thread spindles, and more than 2,300 workers who depend on it for their livelihoods. The occurrence of this incident caused the industry to feel like "a rabbit dies, and a fox grieves," and the general public ran around calling for help. The already uneasy market was further burdened with a greater sense of unease. Although this matter has now been alleviated, the hearts of the industrial and commercial sectors are still filled with anxiety, as if a great disaster is imminent, forming a tragic scene of "the mountain rain is about to come, and the wind fills the building."

Analysis Report on Causes and Consequences

If we carefully consider this uneasy phenomenon in the industrial and commercial sectors from the perspective of this city, the entire country, and the world, we will feel that the current situation is indeed very serious. The recent bankruptcies of a few banks and stores, and the auction of a yarn factory, are only the beginning of this serious situation. If this continues without measures to eliminate it, it will inevitably lead to a total collapse of the entire industry. This is not only a crisis for Shanghai, but also a critical juncture for the survival of the entire nation. Today, I take this opportunity to give you an analysis report on the causes of this serious situation and its possible consequences. Speaking of the causes of this serious situation, some are long-standing, some are recent, some are external, and some are internal. These distant causes, recent causes, external causes, and internal causes are all intertwined and complex, making it difficult to explain them independently.

External Causes: Global Economic Panic

First, let's talk about the external causes. If we go back further, we can explain the impact of all the unequal treaties established after the Opium War and the Treaty of Nanjing on industry and commerce. However, due to the length of the discussion, I will not discuss it here. Now, I will only talk about the recent ones, which must mention the outbreak of the global economic panic in 1929. Since that year, the panic has become increasingly acute. In particular, to mention a few things that are closely related to us, there is the successive abandonment of the gold standard by Britain and Japan in 1931, the abandonment of the gold standard by the United States in 1933, and the vigorous implementation of the silver policy by the United States in 1934. At the same time, the tariff barriers of various countries have become increasingly strict. The so-called "locked country economy" (the economic group of nationalism (Bloc economy) including controlled trade, managed currency, etc., are all universally popular, and there are very concrete and precise methods to implement these policies. China, which has an open door and is backward in everything, is not qualified to join their economic groups, and it seems that there is no way to discuss controlled trade quota allocation with them. Under this situation, the fact that is manifested is that our country's exported goods are either actually prohibited from being imported because they cannot bear the burden of foreign tariffs, or they are everywhere because the purchasing power of foreign markets is low, or foreigners love to use domestic products, or they are replaced by similar goods from other countries. Except for those who have no choice but to purchase our goods, I am afraid that they will not easily absorb other people's money. Looking back at the situation of foreign goods coming to China, what is the situation? Of course, foreign goods are selling well in China, and of course they have their favorable support. For example, as mentioned earlier, the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan have all stopped the gold standard, and the value of their currencies has decreased. At the same time, the exchange rate of our country's currency has naturally fallen. This is why we have cheap foreign goods to enjoy, and their governments also use all kinds of methods, such as exempting export taxes and giving preferential rewards, to help goods be dumped in China. Moreover, within China, there are foreign factories that use our abundant raw materials and labor, plus their strong capital and spiritual technology, so why worry that their products have no market? Therefore, the source of our livelihood for clothing, food, housing, and transportation is already relying on foreign goods. Other unnecessary luxury goods, cosmetics, and even daily necessities that can be replaced by domestic goods are also purchased with foreign goods. Just speaking of the six years from 1929 to the present, the trade deficit in our purchase of foreign goods was the largest in the year before last, reaching 900 million yuan, and the smallest last year was also more than 500 million yuan. Calculating an average of 600 million yuan, the total is 3.6 billion yuan. So much money has flowed out in six years. Everyone, close your eyes and think about it. What a dangerous image this is.

Huge Trade Deficit: The Situation is Serious

This huge trade deficit did not begin in recent years, but it was not considered so serious before, because although trade had a deficit before, it did not require cash to compensate. There was still a cash surplus every year, because there was a large amount of invisible income, such as remittances from overseas Chinese and foreign investment in our country, etc. In recent years, the situation has changed greatly. The careers of overseas Chinese are declining everywhere, and batches of unemployed people are returning to the country, increasing domestic unrest. Foreign investment has of course decreased sharply. Therefore, the current trade deficit must be paid with cash shipments. In addition, after the United States implemented its silver policy last year, overseas silver prices soared. General foreign merchants, banks, and unscrupulous Chinese people are shipping cash overseas for profit. In total, the net outflow of silver last year reached more than 248 million yuan. During this period, although the financial authorities announced on October 15 last year that they would increase the silver export tax and balance tax, and set up a foreign exchange stabilization committee, there was still an outflow of more than 11 million yuan of silver in November and December. According to a survey at the end of December last year, the total silver reserves of Chinese and foreign banks in this city were only more than 33 million yuan. If the outflow continues like that, it will not take long to be emptied.

Internal Causes: The Impact of Rural Bankruptcy

The above are all external causes. Now let's talk about the internal causes. First of all, we must talk about rural bankruptcy. Regarding this matter, there have been many records in recent newspapers and magazines. Many of you present here come from the countryside. Everyone already knows the truth about rural bankruptcy recently, so there is no need to elaborate. I will only point out how rural bankruptcy affects urban decline. Originally, agriculture, industry, and commerce are mutually dependent and cannot thrive independently. Even a large industrial country like the United States can cause economic panic due to agricultural decline. What's more, we are a country based on agriculture. In the past, rural silkworm cocoons, rice, wheat, and cotton were brought to Shanghai to exchange for money and buy industrial products back. Now the silk industry has been completely defeated. Rice, wheat, and cotton are also mostly purchased with foreign goods, amounting to more than 200 million yuan a year. Even the farmers themselves are eating foreign rice. May I ask how many customers are left for urban industrial products? In addition, continuous natural and man-made disasters, such as the national flood in 1931, and the locusts, droughts, and bandits in various places in various years, and the unprecedented national disasters of the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, have eroded an unknown amount of vitality. The losses are difficult to calculate in numbers. These natural and man-made disasters have accelerated the promotion of rural bankruptcy, and have made many inland cities with agriculture as their background increasingly empty, gradually concentrating all their wealth in the cities to seek security, thus forming the phenomenon of urban congestion and inland anemia.

The Consequences in the Future are Unthinkable

Above, I have said a lot about the causes and current situation of the panic in Shanghai. Now let's talk about the future outcome. However, no one can predict what form the future will eventually change into. If we infer from the current situation, there are several points that can be said about the results: 1. Foreign economic self-defense measures will definitely become more sophisticated day by day, and it will be even more difficult for our goods to find a way out abroad. 2. Foreign goods will continue to come in, and the price may decrease, and the price will be lower in order to seek small profits but quick turnover, because the purchasing power of the Chinese people will reach the point where the oil is dry and the lamp wick is exhausted. This trend has been obvious last year. 3. Cash will continue to flow out non-stop, because the United States' silver purchase policy has a consistent direction. Since the Golden Bar Document was adjudicated, currency inflation has become more and more powerful, and silver will be purchased in large quantities according to the planned steps in the future, and its price will inevitably be raised further. 4. Currency contraction, price decline, rural bankruptcy, urban decline, foreign goods import, and domestic product stagnation are all mutually causal and increasingly profound in a cycle. A total collapse of industry is not impossible. 5. A recent survey shows that the number of unemployed people in this city has doubled compared to a year ago, but there is no doubt that the number of unemployed people will continue to increase in the future. Social unrest is a serious problem. I still remember more than ten years ago, when Sun Yat-sen spoke of nationalism, he mentioned the outflow of money and loudly warned us, "If the Chinese people do not wake up again, if this continues, even if foreign politicians are sleeping every day, the country will perish in less than ten years." The current situation is just as Sun Yat-sen showed us ten years later, and today foreign political and economic aggression are proceeding in tandem.

Adversity Strengthens the Nation: Strive Without Slackening

Everyone, what I have said today is all based on facts and is not alarmist. As the saying goes, "Adversity strengthens the nation." We should take advantage of this time of crisis to follow President Chiang Kai-shek's instructions to work hard, work quickly, and work practically, and strive without slackening. I believe that there is great hope for the revival of the nation. Now President Chiang Kai-shek, President Wang, Minister Kong, former Minister Song, Minister Chen, and Mayor Wu have ways to save the current national economic crisis. I hope that the industrial and commercial sectors and the financial community will think about the overall situation and maintain the status quo with the spirit of past cooperation, and help the government to overcome the difficulties together. We must know that only by working together with one heart can we coexist and prosper. As for us, we should be hardworking and enduring, frugal, and wear domestic products uniformly, and implement a new life, and use our personal intelligence and talents to the best of our ability to work for saving the country and survival. We must not be discouraged by the current situation, and we must not abandon the fundamentals and pursue the trivial, and abandon the right path and not go out. We believe that our country has such a large land and so many people, as long as we are of one heart and one mind, and are good at using it, no matter how excellent foreign political and economic constructions are, we will naturally be able to catch up.

Various Public Organizations Request the Banking and Financial Sectors to Maintain Shenxin No. 7 Factory 100

The Second Creditor Agrees with the Government's Intentions

According to the Central News Agency, since the Shenxin Textile Company's No. 7 Factory was arbitrarily valued and auctioned off by the British HSBC Bank, it has aroused widespread resentment in our society. Yesterday morning, the China Industrial Relief Association, the Shanghai Patriotic Goods Promotion Association, the China National Goods Maintenance Association, the Shanghai General Labor Union, the China Industrial Federation, the National Goods Factory Federation, the Machine-made National Goods Factory Federation, the Industrial and Commercial Management Association, and more than 160 trade associations such as flour and miscellaneous grains jointly sent a letter to the Banking and Financial Industry Associations, requesting them to properly raise funds to maintain it. A Central News Agency reporter visited all parties concerned yesterday and said that since HSBC has expressed that there is a possibility of reversing the situation, the final solution still needs to wait for Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi to come to Shanghai before there is a solution. Rong Zongjing, General Manager of Shenxin Textile Company, said that he does not intend to speak out too much in the future to avoid causing additional problems. On the second creditor side, a spokesman for the Bank of China said that future progress should be based on the government's intentions. If the government can redeem the No. 7 factory with its strength (obtain the status of the first creditor) and can share the debts of the second creditor, it is especially agreeable. According to another rumor, if the No. 7 factory can be redeemed by the government's power, it may be handed over to the Cotton Industry Control Association for handling. Since the establishment of the association, although many plans have been proposed, they have not been implemented. Now there is this opportunity, it should be able to show its effectiveness and serve as a model for Chinese yarn factories. However, this statement remains to be verified.

Mayor Wu Instructed Him to Fulfill His Responsibilities

Director Cai Replied That He Would Work Hard at His Duties

Cai Jinjun, the newly appointed Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau of this city, went to the Municipal Government in the city center district yesterday morning at 10:00 after reporting to the bureau on the 1st of this month to participate in the Municipal Government's expanded memorial week and hold a supplementary swearing-in ceremony. Mayor Wu personally supervised the oath. The details are recorded as follows:

Participating People

Those who participated included Mayor Wu, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Director of Security Yang Hu, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Wu Xingya, Director of the Health Bureau Li Tingan, Director of the Public Works Bureau Shen Junyi, the newly appointed Director of the Public Security Bureau Cai Jinjun, and all staff members of the Municipal Government's various offices and bureaus, as well as Xu Jinyuan, Chief of Staff of the Songhu Garrison Command, Wu Shaozeng, Deputy Director of the Two-Roads Administration Bureau, Dong Chongshan of the Gaoer Branch, and Jiang Huaisu, Secretary-General of the Municipal Party Department, and more than a thousand other people.

Oath and Instructions

The Municipal Public Security Bureau specially dispatched a military band to play music at the venue, and additional sentry police were dispatched in front of the Municipal Government. At 10:00 a.m., the guests and staff members who participated in the ceremony had arrived at the venue and sat in rows. Mayor Wu then accompanied the newly appointed Director of the Public Security Bureau Cai Jinjun, Secretary Yu, Director Yang, etc., to the auditorium amidst the music of the military band and took seats in the front row. The ceremony began immediately. After the ceremony was performed as usual, Director Cai Jinjun read the oath, and Mayor Wu supervised the oath. Then Mayor Wu delivered instructions, and Director Cai delivered a reply. At the end, Director Wu Xingya gave a work report, and the ceremony ended and the meeting adjourned.

Mayor's Instructions

Mayor Wu's instructions briefly stated, "Distinguished guests, colleagues, today Director Cai is here to hold a supplementary swearing-in ceremony. Director Cai has worked at the Nanchang Camp in the past and has been directly taught by President Chiang Kai-shek on a daily basis. This time, he has come to Shanghai to take on the position of Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. We deeply believe that Director Cai will definitely be able to fulfill his duties for the public security of this city with his past spirit of hard work and service. Therefore, the colleagues of this government deeply believe that we will definitely be able to get very good help in the future. The people can also firmly believe that Director Cai will have perfect achievements for the public security of this city in the future. In short, we hope that Director Cai will abide by national laws and regulations and obey the orders of superiors in the future in order to fulfill his responsibilities."

Director Cai's Speech

Director Cai then replied, "Jinjun was ordered to take over as Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau on the 1st of this month. Today, at the Municipal Government's expanded memorial week, I am holding a supplementary swearing-in ceremony. I am honored that Mayor Wu has personally supervised the oath and given earnest instructions on the future direction of work. There is something to follow in future work. Although Jinjun has served in senior military agencies for many years in the past, he does not have a deep experience in police administration. This time, I have been ordered to take on the heavy responsibility of Shanghai's public security. In the future, I can only try my best to follow the central government's intentions, follow the Mayor's instructions, and work hard and earnestly in order to live up to the government's entrustment. President Chiang Kai-shek once instructed on the day the Wuchang Camp was established that banning drugs and promoting the New Life Movement are the most important plans for saving the country at present. Based on this principle, Jinjun believes that the most important thing to pay attention to in handling the public security of this city at present is, in the negative aspect, to maintain public order, and banning drugs is also an important matter; in the positive aspect, to strictly implement the New Life Movement and change social customs. Moreover, Shanghai is an international commercial port, which is related to the reputation of the country. If public order cannot be maintained, the people will not be able to live and work in peace. Not only will industrial and commercial undertakings be unable to prosper, but education and culture will also be unable to develop. If the bad social customs are not changed, the foundation for national revival cannot be established, and all construction preparations will not help the country's danger. Therefore, during Jinjun's swearing-in ceremony, in addition to personally swearing to be loyal and serve the country, I also hope that the Mayor will supervise me from time to time, and social leaders and colleagues of this government will assist me at any time so that I can complete this arduous task in order to achieve the government's expectation of prosperity in Shanghai."

Original Text of the Oath

I solemnly swear that I will恪遵 Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, obey the party's meaning, abide by laws, and devote my loyalty and efforts to my duties. I am determined not to waste a single penny, use a single person improperly, and I am determined not to engage in private gain, bribery, or accept bribes. If I violate my oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This oath is made by Cai Jinjun, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, March 4, 1935.

Persia Renamed Iran 103

Name Change Effective March 21

Historical Research on the Meaning of Renaming

The Persian Empire will be officially renamed the Iranian Empire from March 21, 1935, because March 21 is the Iranian New Year. The Persian Consulate in Shanghai announced the reasons for changing the country's name to Iran yesterday, claiming that Persia's original name was Iran, which originated from the Aryan race, which first lived on the Iranian plateau. According to the research of the Greek historian Herodotus, Iran once had a province of Bass, and in the province of Bass, there was a city of Cyrus, named Persepolis, and Persia gradually became used by the whole country and government, and the name Iran was forgotten, and finally the country was named Persia until today. The government has now decided to officially restore the country's name to Iran.

Four Provinces Farmers Bank's Shanghai Branch Decides to Issue Subsidiary Currency Notes 107

One-Dime and Two-Dime Denominations to be Issued Soon

Shanghai Funding of $250,000 No Longer a Problem

According to the New News Agency, the Shanghai branch of the Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi Four Provinces Farmers Bank has seen considerable business growth since its opening. In order to facilitate financial circulation, it plans to issue one-dime and two-dime subsidiary currency notes along the Beijing-Shanghai railway line. The $250,000 in funding for the bank, previously ordered by Chairman Chiang to be raised by the Shanghai Municipal Government, is no longer a problem. A reporter from the New News Agency yesterday inquired about the situation at the bank and reports the details as follows:

Change of Bank Name

The capital of the Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi Four Provinces Farmers Bank is $10 million, with $2.75 million already paid up. Its purpose is to provide funding to farmers, revitalize the rural economy, promote agricultural production, and advocate rural cooperation. Therefore, its business differs somewhat from that of ordinary banks, as its focus is entirely on the farmers. The head office is located in Hankou, with branches established in Hankou, Kaifeng, Zhengzhou, Huangchuan, Yichang, Shashi, Laohekou, Anqing, Wuhu, Liu'an, Nanchang, Jiujiang, Fuzhou, Hukou, Xi'an, Fuzhou Xiahang Street, Fuzhou City, Xiamen, Nanjing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, and other locations. The bank's business is currently developing rapidly, and it plans to establish branches outside the four provinces. However, the existing name of "Four Provinces" is no longer applicable, so it plans to change its name to the China Farmers Bank, which should be realized soon.

Issuance of Subsidiary Currency Notes

According to a spokesman for the bank to the New News Agency reporter, in addition to the one-dollar, five-dollar, and ten-dollar banknotes already issued in the four provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi, one-dime and two-dime subsidiary currency notes have also been issued in Fuzhou, Hangzhou, and other places. The Shanghai branch has now decided to issue one-dime and two-dime subsidiary currency notes along the Beijing-Shanghai railway line in order to facilitate financial circulation. These subsidiary currency notes have already been printed and will be issued on a fixed date as soon as they are shipped from the head office. In the future, one-dollar, five-dollar, and ten-dollar banknotes will be issued as needed.

Fundraising

The bank's total capital is $10 million, with $2.75 million already paid up. Chairman Chiang, believing that the bank's purpose is entirely to promote the farmers' economy, previously ordered the provincial and municipal governments to raise $250,000 in funding. The Shanghai Municipal Government also received this order.

Li Jingcong Discusses the New Construction Department Director's Arrival in the East 108

Negotiating the Resumption of the Shanghai-Xinjiang Air Route

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai-Xinjiang air route of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation has been repeatedly postponed due to the unrest and instability in Xinjiang Province, and has not been able to open. Yesterday, according to Li Jingcong, general manager of the company, to the Central News Agency reporter, Gao Xibing, the newly appointed Director of the Construction Department of Xinjiang Province, has come to the east to find a concrete solution for the resumption of the air route. The details are as follows:

Xinjiang Representative Negotiating Resumption of Flights

According to Li, the Northwest air route of the Eurasia Company is a shortcut to connect Europe and Asia. Unfortunately, the civil war in the province has interrupted the plan for joint flights for years. Sheng Shicai previously telegraphed Executive Yuan President Wang, stating that the area was now peaceful and requesting that personnel be sent to make arrangements. The company authorities approved his request and are preparing to send personnel there this month. Now that Director Gao of the Construction Department of the province has also come east, after detailed consultations with him, they can begin to resume flights.

South Asia Route Not Needed

It does not seem necessary to open a South Asia air route, and the expenses and various procedures are quite inconvenient. The most important thing for connecting European and Asian aviation is the convenience of mail. Today, mail to Europe can be forwarded via Siberia, which only takes twelve days to reach Europe. Opening a South Asia air route would also take the same amount of time. The most convenient way is to go directly through Xinjiang, which only takes five or six days. Therefore, instead of talking about opening a South Asia air route, it is better to focus on resuming the Shanghai-Xinjiang air route.

Building Hangar at Longhua Airport

Since the Eurasia Company moved its airport to Longhua, it has been easy to damage the aircraft when landing and parking in the open field. Therefore, it has been decided to build its own hangar for parking. According to Li, the drawings have already been completed, and the funding is also in place. A board meeting will be held in the coming days to discuss it, and once a formal decision is made, bidding will be invited for construction.

Business Booming Since Price Reduction

In order to provide convenience for passengers, the company has launched a three-month price reduction program last month. It is understood that the business on all routes, except for mail, is very prosperous, which is very different from before the price reduction. As for the combined transport with land and sea, although it is intended to facilitate transportation, the company does not see an urgent need for it in practice, so it will not be realized in the short term.

Ministry of Finance Orders Money Shops Not to Discriminate Against Dime Coins 112

Money Shops Guild Issues Public Notice After Receiving Order

And Sends Letter to Tobacco and Exchange Guild to Comply

The Shanghai Money Shops Guild received an order from the Ministry of Finance Qianzi No. 12574, which stated, "The Executive Yuan Secretariat's letter on the case opened, ordered by the President, submitted by the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Special Party Department, regarding (omitted) the long-standing discrimination by money shops in Beijing and Shanghai against dime coins from the 7th to the 10th years of the Republic, mutually refusing to accept them or suppressing their exchange value. Although local administrative agencies have issued public notices to ban this practice, this trend has subsided slightly in recent years, but those who exchange coins still cannot avoid adhering to old habits, discriminating against dime coins, and suppressing exchange rates in order to profit from them, deceiving the common people. It is urgent to strictly prohibit this again in order to prevent manipulation and stabilize the market. In addition to informing the Shanghai and Nanjing Municipal Governments to issue public notices to ban this practice, you are hereby ordered to comply and instruct all money shops not to discriminate against dime coins from the 7th to the 10th years of the Republic and to temporarily allow them to be used in the market until new subsidiary coins are formulated and promulgated. This order." After receiving the order, the guild issued a public notice and sent a letter to the Tobacco and Exchange Guild to comply.

Organizational Methods of Various Marketing Cooperatives 113

Mr. Stephen is an American marketing cooperative expert. This time, he was hired by Jinling University to lecture on agricultural product marketing cooperation at the university. He previously lectured on various cooperation issues multiple times at the Shanghai Bank Agricultural Cooperation Lecture Hall. Mr. Stephen has rich experience in marketing cooperation. His proposals are indeed an important reference for those in our country who are engaged in and studying marketing cooperation. This article is based on Mr. Stephen's lecture at the bank's agricultural cooperation lecture hall on the morning of February 12, translated by Professor Xu Zhongdi, and recorded by Cheng Mi and Zhu Yaqiang. The original manuscript is reproduced below.

There are many things to pay attention to regarding marketing cooperatives. Among them, the organizational methods of various marketing cooperatives are the most important. The relationship between various cooperatives, the completeness of the organization of each cooperative itself, and whether its method is appropriate are sufficient to affect the success or failure of the cooperative. The organization and management of a cooperative are like a ship at sea, which requires not only a strong hull, but also an experienced captain to manage it. Both must be available in order to sail safely.

A. Prerequisites for the Branch Organization of a Marketing Cooperative (1) The branches of a marketing cooperative should be located in natural areas where agricultural products are concentrated. Therefore, the scope and location of marketing cooperatives are different from those of credit cooperatives. The matters handled by the branches are illustrated by cotton, which includes procedures such as collecting seed cotton, grading, ginning, baling, stacking, storing, and transporting. If taking fruits as an example, it includes procedures such as collecting fruits, washing fruits, inspecting and selecting fruits, grading, packaging, and boxing. Other cooperatives such as tobacco and tea have similar procedures. Therefore, the site must be located in a place where agricultural products are concentrated. (2) The regional scope of marketing cooperatives should not be too small. Because the above-mentioned procedures must have considerable equipment and expenses. If the scope is too small and the agricultural products are too few, it will increase the cost of equipment management and operation required for each unit of agricultural product. However, it should not be too large, because it is not easy for members to deliver agricultural products, which will inevitably affect the cooperative's equipment, budget, and business volume, resulting in inaccurate estimates and increased costs. As for marketing issues, the marketing cooperative may not be able to handle them, and a union should be organized by the branches to handle marketing issues.

B. Organization of the Marketing Cooperative Union The function of the union is to handle the marketing of the products of the branch members. Therefore, there is no need for the union to have processing equipment like the cooperative. The union only creates effective advertising and tries to sell to major city markets. For example, the American Cotton Cooperative Association and the California Fruit Growers Exchange are both union-style organizations. The cooperatives under the latter only handle procedures such as receiving fruits, washing fruits, grading, and packaging. The work of the union's headquarters is to find ways to sell, and to take necessary advertising propaganda and business policies.

C. Organization of Centralized Marketing Cooperatives Centralized cooperatives are different from unions. Each small platform cooperative in the union is independent and can withdraw from the headquarters at any time. However, centralized cooperatives cannot. The members of centralized cooperatives are widely distributed, and their directors are elected separately by the members of each region. In addition to executing the central authority of the entire society, the cooperative's board of directors also manages various businesses in each district of the society, and sets up packaging, grading, and other matters in each district, all of which are transferred according to the intentions of the central agency.

D. Comparison of Union and Centralized Types The policies and management of centralized cooperatives are based solely on the intentions of the manager, who can notify the offices in each district to comply by means of orders, without the consent of the members of each district. This kind of management, if the method is good, is convenient to manage, easy to use, and can achieve rapid results. However, this is not the case with the union-type cooperative, which cannot implement a command-style management policy, but can only guide and explain from the sidelines, and is only advisory in nature. The union's responsibility is only to promote sales, and all other procedures are freely handled by the branches. If the union has new policies and new methods, it can only advise the branches to implement them, and each branch must adopt them after the approval of the board of directors. This is the difference between the centralized and union-type cooperatives. (To be continued)

China and Other Five Banks Invest in Jiangsu Province Commodity Marketing Cooperative 114

Inland Industrial and Commercial Enterprises Can Obtain Agents in Shanghai

Other Provinces Willing to Support If They Follow Suit

According to the New Sound News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, in order to rescue industry and commerce and prosper the market, has established the Shanghai Commodity Marketing Trust Company, with an investment of one million yuan from China and other five banks, and a general office has been established in Shanghai to purchase commodities. The details are as follows:

Establishment of Trust Company Director Zhao Dihua of the Department of Finance, in view of the unusual decline of various industries in Jiangsu Province, in order to rescue industry and commerce and prosper the market, has planned to establish the Shanghai Commodity Marketing Trust Company, and invited China Communications, Shanghai Jiangsu Farmers and other five banks to jointly invest. It has been successfully contacted with the Zhenjiang branches of various banks, and the total investment is one million yuan, which will be used as the capital of the trust company. It has been decided to establish a general office in Shanghai and a branch office in Zhenjiang.

Classification of Business The business of the Shanghai Commodity Marketing Trust Company is: (1) acting as an agent for inland industrial and commercial enterprises to purchase commodities and raw materials in Shanghai; (2) handling mortgage loans and remittances for commodities and raw materials transported to the inland; (3) handling packaging, transportation, insurance, and customs declaration for commodities and raw materials transported to the inland; (4) introducing and promoting various commodities of the industrial and commercial community; (5) acting as an agent to investigate market conditions and supply market information. Those who entrust purchases must first pay 20% of the price. The commission charged is no more than 3%, of which 30% is used as a bonus and the remainder is used as a public reserve fund.

Bank Support The New Sound News Agency reporter yesterday learned from the banking community that they all agreed with the Jiangsu Province Shanghai Commodity Marketing Trust Company. However, the company's accounting is supervised by the investing banks. They have infinite hope for reviving industry and commerce and prospering the market. If other places follow the Jiangsu Province approach, the banks will do their best to help.

China and Foreign Relief Association's Jiangning Six Counties Face Severe Spring Famine 119

The China and Foreign Relief Association on Renji Road said that the area affected by the drought last year was too large to be supported by its own strength. For the relief of Jiangning and other counties, it could only jointly organize with other charitable organizations to carry out emergency work and conduct relief step by step. Except for the two counties of Liuhe and Jiangning, because the funds had been fully allocated and nothing was left, the disaster relief work was still not enough. According to the disaster area reports, the relief work in Jiangpu, Jurong, Lishui, and Gaochun has been reported that because the wheat season is still far away, there is a shortage of food, and the general disaster victims are in a precarious situation. Now, with the approval to preside over the disaster relief work, Ling Jundao Yang of the Ning Agricultural Relief Association said in a letter that the disaster in (Liuhe) is unique among several counties. Its total area of farmland is 830,000 mu, and the total population is 357,221. The disaster-stricken farmland accounts for 80%, totaling 684,000 mu, and the disaster victims account for about 75%, reaching 269,400 people. According to the field survey, the hungry people are eating grass roots and tree bark. The cultivated fields are willing to put up a mortgage of two yuan per mu, but no one cares. (Jiangning) has a farmland area of 1.43 million mu and a total population of 422,878. The disaster-stricken farmland accounts for about 70%, totaling more than 997,000 mu, and the disaster victims account for 45%, reaching more than 200,000 people. Now that it is the spring famine, they are going out to find food, wandering around, and dying of hunger. People know the vanity of the city, but unfortunately they do not know the poverty of the countryside. How can they bear to feel regret for nothing? As for (Jiangpu), during this spring famine, selling children and eating beef are often heard. (Jurong) The people's livelihood is becoming more and more difficult. The young and strong are doing hard labor, eating from door to door, fleeing famine, and robbing. The old and weak are begging, selling their children, and committing suicide. In short, 97% of the farmers in the whole county are using Guanyin flour, barnyard grass flour, and yam to fill their stomachs. (Lishui) has long been a scorched earth with no life at all. It is not uncommon to see people hanging themselves or starving to death. (Gaochun) has more than 2,000 square miles of red land, with 156,000 disaster victims. Chickens and pigs are sold cheaply and nothing remains. They are now destitute, wandering on the road, and there are dead bodies in the wild. All of these are rare and tragic situations in the world. I think good-hearted gentlemen, concerned about this, will not be able to eat, and I hope to add help to my family. Otherwise, the relief in winter will not help in spring, and the success will fall short, which is really unbearable.

Chung Hwa Book Company Compiles and Prints Junior High School Students' Library 125

The extracurricular reading materials for students of all levels of schools have become a serious problem in the education sector in recent years. Although publishers are trying their best to supply them, most of them are for elementary school students. Those that are available for extracurricular reading for secondary school students are mostly too advanced and can only meet the needs of high school students. No one has taken into account the junior high school students who are between high school and elementary school. Recently, in order to meet this need, Chung Hwa Book Company has specially compiled a junior high school student library, which contains 255 kinds of books, totaling 200 volumes. Among them, there are those that provide students with learning methods, such as learning methods for various subjects, table explanations for various subjects, mathematical problems, solutions, guidance, research, etc.; there are those that supplement the lack of textbook knowledge, such as biographies, travel notes, applied science, and shallow explanations of various subjects, etc.; there are those that provide students with the cultivation of life skills, such as planting, animal husbandry, housework, and hygiene, etc.; there are those that provide students with the appreciation of literature and art, such as selected annotated versions of Chinese and English literature, etc.; and there are those that assist in civic training, such as military affairs, national defense, self-cultivation, and vocational guidance, etc. All of these books are compiled by experts and middle school teachers according to their strengths and in accordance with the subjects and levels of junior high school students, without being too lofty or impractical, and with a systematic and interesting approach. Junior high school students who purchase this book can get access to the learning methods of various subjects and arouse their interest in learning various subjects. Schools can also solve the difficulty of selecting extracurricular reading materials by preparing this book. Even elementary school graduates who aspire to further their studies or those who are taking part-time remedial classes can also get rid of the difficulty of finding reading materials. The library is priced at 80 yuan, but is now on sale for half price, only 40 yuan. Those who pay in four installments will pay 44 yuan, that is, 11 yuan each time. Pre-orders will be closed at the end of April, and the entire set will be published in four installments starting from the end of June this year. This is truly good news for secondary school students.

Rare Edition of Water Margin Falls into the Hands of the Japanese 126

Only Two Copies Exist in the World

According to the Japanese Shanghai Daily News, the Four Great Classical Novels of Chinese literature, Romance of the Three Kingdoms, Journey to the West, Jin Ping Mei, and Water Margin, are among the world's masterpieces. Among them, the rare edition of Water Margin in 100 chapters, criticized by Zhong Bojing, only has two copies in the world. One is stored in the National Library of France in Paris, and the other is the one recently donated by Mr. Kamiya Junji, a guard of the Jinkeima, to the Kyoto Imperial University Library. It is said that there are originally six kinds of Water Margin. The one that is usually known is the popular edition of 120 chapters sold in the market. There are also editions of 70 chapters, 100 chapters, and 50 chapters. Among these types, the 100-chapter edition is the most accurate. Decades ago, China searched for it without success. Unexpectedly, the book has fallen into the hands of Dr. Shi Yan Guwen, an authority in the field of study. The book has no illustrations. The most regrettable thing is that the first page is missing. It is a Ming edition, but the year is unknown. However, on the third page of the twenty-second chapter, there are the words "Jiqingtang Collection." In the future, it should be possible to clarify its system and origin. However, the reason why this book cannot be found in China is due to the disaster of the Qing government's policy of burning books. It is said that the popular edition in the market was compiled by Shi Nai'an of the Yuan Dynasty, and its content and number of chapters are very different from this rare edition.

According to Guomin News Agency, Feng Deyuan, courtesy name Zhiqing, from Wuxian County, is 45 years old. His son, Genbo, told reporters that he has been searching for days without any news and will go to Putuo or Hangzhou temples to find him. Otherwise, he is unwilling to live alone in the world. The reporter saw the situation and felt pity. If Mr. Feng's relatives and friends can know his whereabouts and inform him to save his family, it would be a great merit. Shanghai National Goods Company Establishes a Mutual Aid Market to Promote National Goods 134

Shanghai National Goods Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, is aware that the economic panic is becoming increasingly serious. In fact, although national goods, industry and commerce have been hit, it is also an opportunity for national goods, industry and commerce to unite and fight together. In order to call for the cooperation of the national goods industry, the company has now formulated a method for setting up a mutual aid market to promote national goods based on the principle of mutual benefit, in order to assist national goods products and promote sales. This is indeed good news in the midst of sluggish national goods sales. The method is recorded as follows: The Shanghai National Goods Company, the person who establishes the mutual aid contract, (hereinafter referred to as Party A and Party B) Now Party A initiates the establishment of a market to promote national goods and various national goods factories, and the two parties implement cooperation. The terms and conditions are agreed as follows: (1) Party A designates a suitable place for Party B to display all its products. (2) Party B must fully provide good products for sale, and the price must be based on the cost and must not be raised. The goods must be verified and registered by Party A before entering the market. (3) Party A is responsible for providing appropriate lighting and appropriate advertising and publicity. (4) Party B may send a number of good employees to the mutual aid market to serve, pay their own salaries, obey the unified command of Party A, and Party A provides two meals a day, morning and evening. (5) A few percent of Party B's products sold will be pre-deducted to subsidize Party A. (6) The mutual aid period is fixed for a few days. With the consent of both parties, it can be renewed. (7) The settlement is made once upon the expiration of the term, and the remaining money will be paid to Party B by Party A as a whole. A receipt must be issued separately for receiving the money. (8) After the expiration date, if Party B is unwilling to take back the remaining goods, it will be regarded as consignment goods, and the employees received will be settled and withdrawn on the same day. (9) If there are any matters not covered in each clause of this agreement, they may be negotiated and handled at any time. (10) This mutual aid contract is in duplicate, and each party holds one copy. The legal representative of the mutual aid contract established on the day, month, and year, the legal representative.

French Soldier Wounds British Soldier with Gun 142

Dancing Hall Accident

The Great American Evening News reports that on Saturday night last week, British Navy sailor Cochrane of the HMS Grimsby, along with his friend Baldwin, went to the Crystal Dancing Hall on Rue Chu Pao-san in the French Concession to enjoy dancing. His dance partner was a Russian dancer, and the two were very intimate, which ignited the jealousy of Ponsard, a sergeant in the French Colonial Army infantry who had feelings for the dancer. Around 4:00 AM on Sunday morning, as the dancing hall closed and Cochrane and his friend exited, Ponsard took advantage of their unpreparedness and shot at them, the bullet hitting Cochrane in the head. He immediately fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Seeing his objective achieved, the assailant fled. Cochrane's friend Baldwin gave chase but was ultimately unable to catch him. At this time, patrol officers arrived, disarmed him, and took him into custody. Cochrane was rushed to the Country Hospital, and after surgery performed by naval and civilian surgeons yesterday afternoon, his condition today (the 4th) remains critical. However, hospital staff stated there is hope for recovery. It is reported that the assailant, Ponsard, will be tried by a naval court, and the severity of his punishment will depend on whether Cochrane recovers.

A Hotel Guest at the Yangtze Hotel Exits Covered in Blood 143

After Interrogation by the Detective

It Was Discovered the Dispute Arose From Gambling

Around 4:00 AM the day before yesterday, Xue Zhiwen, the head Chinese detective of the Lao Zha precinct, was patrolling his jurisdiction. At 4:45 AM, while passing the entrance of the Yangtze Hotel on Yunnan Road, he saw Wu Delin, a man from Anhui, exit the hotel covered in blood. Detective Xue stopped him and inquired about the cause of the bleeding. Wu claimed that several Cantonese men had opened a gambling den in room 613 of the hotel, and he had participated in the gambling. It had been going on from around 9:00 PM until the present time. However, half an hour prior, six or seven people dressed in gray suddenly arrived, claiming to be detectives from the police station. They confiscated the cash on the table and on the gamblers, and also took away the pai gow tiles. Everyone gambling inside was Cantonese except for him, an Anhui native. They suspected him of being an informant, so they beat him severely and stabbed him in the head with a knife. Then, they changed rooms to room 311 on the third floor. Detective Xue then led a Chinese police officer to room 311 and arrested nine Cantonese men: Liang Rong, Wang Fei, Zhang De, Deng You, Hu Zhen, Feng San, Chen Sheng, Shi Zhenxiong, and Zhu Qiaosheng. Inside the room, they confiscated a mahjong set, smoking paraphernalia, and two daggers. Then, they went to room 613 and arrested two men from Anhui: Hu Zigao and Fang Deming. At that time, Wang Yingjie and Weng Hongxun, Chinese detectives from the Lao Zha precinct, arrived with a prison wagon. As they were about to put the suspects on the wagon, a Cantonese man named He Hai stepped forward and told the suspects that he could find guarantors for them. The detective suspected He might also be involved and arrested him as well. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special Court's Criminal Division One. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, explained the situation, stating that the case had not yet been fully investigated and requesting permission to detain them temporarily. Judge Feng Shide reviewed the report and ordered a postponement for further questioning.

Theft Case of a St. Anna Dancing Girl 144

Miao Jianpei is Suspected

But No Evidence Was Found

Miao Jianpei, a woman from Wuxi, is twenty-five years old, with a graceful figure and beautiful appearance. She once worked as a dancing girl at the St. Anna Dance Hall. Because of poor health, she quit the embracing lifestyle and settled at number 148 Guling Road, focusing on medical treatment. Now that her health has recovered, to maintain her livelihood, she was recently rehired by St. Anna and resumed her old profession, starting to dance again on Saturday last week (the 2nd). However, according to St. Anna's regulations for managing dancing girls, all dancing girls must dance until 4:00 AM the next morning before being allowed to leave. The dance hall provides a car for transportation. Due to her weakened condition after illness, Miss Miao found it difficult to endure. She felt exhausted after dancing until 3:50 AM the day before yesterday (Sunday). She went to the cloakroom to retrieve her stored coat, handbag, and other items and hired a rickshaw home. Around 4:00 AM, the other dancing girls finished dancing and returned home. However, when the dancing girl Mai Shaoqiong went to Wang Liu, the woman in charge of the cloakroom, to retrieve her stored items, she suddenly discovered that a handbag, containing 40 yuan in dance tickets, 45 yuan in cash, and other cosmetics valued at around 105 yuan, was missing. After a thorough investigation, there were no clues. Wang Liu stated that no one had been there except for the dancing girl Miao Jianpei, who had retrieved her belongings and went home by herself. Therefore, Miao was suspected of being involved in the theft, and the police were notified. Detectives were sent to arrest Miao Jianpei, but a search revealed no stolen goods. Miao was taken to the police station and then to the women's detention center. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the First Special Court's Criminal Division Two. The police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, filed charges for theft, based on the accusation of Wang Liu, a Cantonese woman who was in charge of the cloakroom and bathrooms at the St. Anna Dance Hall. All dancing girls must store their belongings upon entry, which she would keep safe. Around 3:00 AM yesterday morning, the defendant arrived and retrieved her stored items, which she handed over. At the time, another dancing girl came to retrieve her belongings, and she went to another room to fetch them. Later, Mai Shaoqiong suddenly discovered that her handbag was stolen. Since only the defendant was standing in front of the closet at the time, it was certain that the defendant had stolen it. When questioned, Miao Jianpei stated that on Saturday night last week, it was her first time dancing at St. Anna. Because she felt exhausted at 3:50 AM the next morning, she hired a car home herself. Her residence was not far from the dance hall, and the dance hall's transportation car required ten people to ride together, sending people off in segments, which was quite uncomfortable. Therefore, she hired a rickshaw home and did not steal anyone's handbag. She hired lawyer Wu Peng to defend her in court. After Judge Ye Shengchao reviewed the statements, he stated that further investigation of the case was necessary. He ordered Miao Jianpei to provide a reliable guarantor, to be available upon summon and postponed the hearing for seven days.
