Amateur Mailbox

My Father Disappoints Me Too Much 197

Editor:

I now have a difficult problem to solve, and I would like to ask you to guide me to a solution.

A few months ago, I graduated from senior primary school. At that time, I wanted to continue my studies, but my family did not allow me to enter middle school. They wanted to send me to a certain store to be an apprentice to lighten the family’s burden. At that time, for the sake of lifelong happiness, I tried my best to resist, but I had to go to that store because of my father's orders and live that life like a beast of burden.

Now, although I am an apprentice, my enthusiasm for studying has not changed. I very much hope to achieve my desire. So I often beg my family to restore my study life. However, the result is always disappointment! At the same time, my father is very dissatisfied with me because I resisted his opinion and did not listen to him. That stern attitude is really unbearable. Under such circumstances, I developed a bad ideal: I want to break away from the shackles of the family and live independently. First, I think that the reason why I cannot study is entirely due to the oppression of the family. If there is no family to stop me, I may be able to achieve the goal of studying. At the same time, my father's attitude has disappointed me too much.

However, although I have this ideal, I do not have the power to implement it, and how can I leave my kind grandmother and mother? Therefore, I thought about it again and again, and it was really difficult. Dear Sir! How can I fulfill my ambition to study? How can I break away from my family without suffering? Please guide me! Respectfully, Wang Shaogao

Editor's Note: In this year of economic panic, the lives of ordinary people have serious problems. Who has extra money to provide for their children's studies? Therefore, Mr. Wang should first carefully observe whether the family has the ability to continue to provide tuition. If you are prevented from entering school due to economic difficulties, then you must forgive them, because you must never let them starve to death for the sake of your personal studies.

Now you cannot achieve your desire to study, and because of your father's stern attitude, you want to break away from your family. This is a very wrong mentality. May I ask you: After you break away from your family, do you have the ability to study? Can you support yourself now?

As for the reason why your father treats you badly, it is probably because you resisted his opinion. But we think that after his anger subsides, he will still love you. At that time, if you explain the reasons again and beg him to let you study, you may be able to achieve your goal. Because only parents in the world can best forgive their children. Moreover, although your father is now very strict, you still have a kind grandmother and mother. They must be very kind to you. You must not lose your loving family because of temporary indignation!

Regarding the point of studying, we believe that while serving, you are also studying. All practical experience is your knowledge. You can use your spare time to work hard on self-study, and you will definitely make progress over time. Therefore, we advise you not to feel pain and disappointment because you cannot study at school.

If you want to read, you can directly write to the library to inquire about the joining procedures.

Classical Chinese 200

Ms. Wang Bingmei's National Studies

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Duke Zhuang of Zheng Conquers Duan in Yan (Part 2)

Duke Zhuang's plans were not yet over. In the eleventh year of Duke Yin of Lu, Duke Zhuang enfeoffed Xu to his uncle, saying, "I have a brother who cannot live in harmony, and I let him make a living in the four directions. How can he possess Xu for long?" This statement was Duke Zhuang's intention to deceive the world. In the sixteenth year of Duke Zhuang of Lu, Zheng Gongfu, Ding Shu, fled to Wei, and after three years he was restored, saying, "I cannot let Gongshu have no descendants in Zheng." Then Gongshu has descendants in the old Zheng. Duan has descendants, which is Duke Zhuang's intention to deceive later generations. He deceived his court, his state, the world, and later generations. Alas, alas, precarious and dangerous is Duke Zhuang's heart.

To deceive others, one must first deceive one's own heart. Duke Zhuang was only pleased that many people were deceived by him, but he did not know that he deceived his own heart more. The harm of being deceived is harm to the body. The harm of deceiving others is harm to the heart. There is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart, and the death of the body is second. Those who are deceived, although their bodies are harmed, their hearts are still at ease. Those who deceive others, although their bodies achieve their goals, their hearts have been hewn and lost without a trace. What is lost by the former is very light, and what is lost by the latter is very heavy. It is like a fisherman swallowing the bait himself, or a hunter throwing himself into a trap. If not for the most clumsy person in the world, how could one reach this point? Therefore, I initially thought Duke Zhuang was the most dangerous person in the world, but I finally thought Duke Zhuang was the most clumsy person in the world.

Tang's inscription on the plate says, "If you can renovate yourself for one day, then you can renovate yourself every day, and again, you can renovate yourself every day." (The plate is the bath plate. The inscription is to name the vessel with words to warn oneself. Gou means sincerity. Tang uses people's washing their hearts to remove evil, just like bathing their bodies to remove dirt, so he inscribed his plate, saying that if one can sincerely use one day to cleanse the dirt of the old dyeing and renovate oneself, then one should rely on the already new person, and renovate oneself every day, and again, renovate oneself every day, and one must not have any interruptions.) The Kang Gao says, "Create new people." (Gu means dancing and encouraging. It means to revive the self-renovating people.) The poem says, "Zhou, although an old state, its mandate is new." (The poem is a chapter of the Great Elegant Wen Wang, saying that although the Zhou state is old, as for King Wen, he can renew his virtue and extend it to the people and begin to receive the mandate of heaven.)

Shen Bao Local Supplement Architectural Weekly

Architectural Talks 202

— Translated by Chen Hongduo

(1) Manufacturing Method of Hollow Concrete Piles

When building a bridge, the Missouri Pacific Railroad in the United States adopted a new method to manufacture steel-reinforced concrete piles to reduce their weight and obtain greater pile surface friction at the same weight. The cross-section of the pile is octagonal, with a diameter of 24 hours and a hollow diameter of 10 inches. One pile is 36 feet long and has a hollow throughout its length. The opening at the tip is flattened. Another pile has a solid tip, and the straight trunk is hollow, extending to the top of the pile.

When the pile was driven into the last foot, although there were 150 hammer blows, the pile head was not damaged. According to the pile driving records, after a pile was driven in, the soil squeezed into the hollow interior for 14 feet and 8 inches. Before the pile reached the hard stratum, the hammering was much easier than that of a solid concrete pile.

The hollow is made with a retractable rubber tube that expands to the specified diameter by gas or hydraulic power while reducing its length. After the concrete hardens, the rubber tube is pulled out.

(2) New Hollow Roof Concrete Blocks

These blocks are made of asbestos cement, 6 feet long and 2 feet 6 inches wide, and are used for flat roofs or roofs with very small slopes. The blocks are hollow, so they can prevent the transmission of heat and sound. They are not heavy and can be transported by two people.

After the blocks are placed, the horizontal seams are connected to each other, and the vertical seams are filled with cement slurry. If the blocks are placed on trusses, they can also be used as a working platform. Before the oil felt or asphalt is laid on the blocks, a covering roof has been formed, which is enough to prevent rainwater from penetrating, making other work easier and more convenient.

(3) New Fireproof Concrete Floor

This new type of fireproof concrete floor is known for its rapid construction and simple arch frame. Its structure is hollow, with one side closed. When installed, the hollow openings are connected to form 18-inch square blocks, like a sealed box, with a thickness ranging from 4.5 inches to 9 inches. The lower flange of the two parallel sides extends slightly beyond itself. During installation, the flanges of the two blocks are connected, and straight steel bars are placed in the resulting gap. The lower flange of the closed end is also connected in the same way to place horizontal steel bars. These concrete blocks are mostly manufactured on-site.

The arch frame is welded with No. 16 steel plate, and its middle section is triangular, with three sizes to suit different spans. Transportation, installation and dismantling are very convenient. The web of the arch frame is cut off at the end, and the flange retains a 2-inch long and 7.5-inch wide support area to transmit the load to the brick wall or other supports. Each end of the arch frame is left with an empty eye so that a tool can be inserted to pull back its extended part. If the floor is completed, the arch frame can be dismantled.

The special convenience of this arch frame is that it does not require support in the middle, so there is no obstruction under the floor and other work can be carried out.

The center distance of the arch frame is 18 inches. Because of its simplicity, a hundred square yards of floor area can be installed in one sentence. Then, hollow concrete blocks are placed, and horizontal and vertical steel bars are added to the resulting gap, and fine concrete is poured to become ribs. If necessary, another layer of concrete is added on top. After four days, the arch frame can be dismantled according to the aforementioned method. After the blocks are laid, it becomes a working platform, which is very convenient.

Both sides of the board are equipped with steel bars, so the load distribution area is larger and the safety factor is higher. According to the test results, the deflection in the center of a 15-foot span is only one-twentieth of an inch for a floor designed with a load of 100 pounds per square foot, with a weight of 5 tons concentrated in an area of 4 square feet. After the load is removed, the board returns to its original shape. Furthermore, the use of bidirectional steel bars and fewer cracks in the flat top make it more suitable. This type of concrete block does not deform like hollow bricks and is easy to apply mud and whitewash.

The thickness of the blocks can be changed, and the thickness of the concrete layer added on top can also be increased or decreased to suit various floor loads.

Random Talks on Building City Houses in Commercial Areas 203

— Ying Dai

Shop houses or houses in small commercial areas have become extremely important in the construction industry in recent years. Let's take the United States as an example. In the past year, contracts signed by various construction companies show that this type of housing accounted for more than 50%. Although China's commerce is relatively backward, shop houses in urban areas naturally occupy an extremely important position in the construction industry. The rapid changes in shop habits and the rapid development of industry and commerce in recent years have directly and indirectly led to the frequent demolition, construction, or renovation of shop houses.

The form of shops is actively being modernized. As a result, shop houses have to be rebuilt frequently. When building these houses, the metals, glass, wood, and various new building materials used have been widely applied. The lighting in new-style shops is also different from the past. Reflective effects are often used to attract the attention of passersby. Therefore, the renovation and reconstruction of shops and commercial areas is rapidly expanding in major cities. At the same time, the development of industry and commerce has made the current limited number of shops insufficient, which has also led to the construction of new shops and commercial areas.

For the sake of modernizing shops and expanding commercial areas, even small cities are building commercial areas. However, we should also pay attention to the selection of sites before building city houses. The first step is to analyze the local situation. Is this location busy with pedestrians and vehicles? If it is busy, then we can use this site. After the site is found, we should pay attention to the display of goods in the kitchen windows and whether the work area of the staff in the shop is properly arranged. A walkway must be left out naturally. In fact, when building modern shops and shop houses, all work, including carpentry, earthwork, masonry, and plumbing, is different from the past.

Professional architects should take care of everything in the construction of city houses. After the house is built, whether it is suitable for the local environment, how much electricity is supplied by the local electricity company and lighting company, and how electric lights, reflective lights, and New Year's lights should be installed in the shop are all the architect's responsibility to plan. In a city where the population is rapidly increasing, residential areas are naturally expanding with the population. With a large population, the original central market will inevitably be inconvenient to supply all residential areas. Then, second-class markets will naturally be built around the central market. The location of these markets, the environment, and the level of residents in the surrounding residential areas must be considered. If they are all wealthy families, the shop houses must naturally be built more grandly. Conversely, if they are all ordinary people, then it can be more casual.

In recent years, we often hear about fires inside shops in cities. Because of the accumulation of goods in shops, many of them are flammable, so once a fire breaks out, it is irreparable and may even spread to multiple households. Regarding this point, we should pay extra attention to fire prevention when building city houses. If possible, the houses should be built with steel-reinforced concrete, and even doors and windows should be made of steel. Even the escalators should be made of iron railings and stone steps. If this is not possible, then use as little flammable wood as possible. More attention should be paid to fire prevention equipment.

Building Materials (4) 204

— Zhu Zhenmu

Section Five: Testing of Building Materials

The purpose of material testing is to determine the characteristic properties of a material, whether it fully meets all the requirements in the ideal situation, and to determine the criteria for selection or rejection.

There are broadly two approaches to ordinary testing: chemical methods and mechanical methods.

1. Chemical Testing Method: This method can be used to determine the various qualities of the components contained in a small sample, and all kinds of unfavorable and unnecessary impurities can also be detected.

2. Mechanical Testing Method: This method can test the material's force capacity, elasticity, and other material properties described above.

In addition, when we have rich experience, our hands and eyes can also discern and judge the advantages and disadvantages of material properties to some extent, but this is only for convenience and not a proper method.

Chapter Two: Pig Iron

Section One: Iron Ore

Iron ore is a mineral. The pure form of iron ore is a type of iron oxide. Pig iron is produced by removing oxygen from this type of iron ore. The quality of iron ore is determined by the amount of iron it contains. Ore containing 50% or more iron is considered high-grade, while ore containing less than 50% is considered low-grade. Common impurities mixed in iron ore include sulfur, phosphorus, and silicon, all of which are undesirable in pig iron.

Section Two: Manufacturing of Pig Iron

To remove oxygen from iron ore, carbon is used for reduction. This carbon can be obtained from fuel coal. Because iron ore often contains impurities, limestone is also needed as a medium to combine and remove impurities. The manufacturing method involves a blast furnace, coke, limestone, iron ore, and the following steps:

(1) Place pig iron, coke, and limestone into the blast furnace in alternating layers, with the thickness ratio being 3/6 for pig iron, 3/8 for coke, and 1/8 for limestone. The furnace temperature must be 1000 degrees Fahrenheit.

(2) Blow cold air into the furnace from the bottom, with a pressure of about 15 pounds per square inch.

(3) The carbon in the coke then absorbs oxygen and turns into carbon monoxide, which then combines with the hot oxygen in the iron ore to form carbon dioxide, causing the pig iron to sink to the bottom of the furnace and flow out.

(4) Impurities in the ore combine with limestone to form slag, which floats on the surface of the furnace.

Releasing gas once per hour, if we consider the consumption of 1000 tons of iron ore, 500 tons of coke, 300 tons of limestone, and 2000 tons of air, 500 tons of pig iron can be produced every six hours. (To be continued)

Construction Jargon (6) 205

— Mei Zhenhuan

Terms Used on the Construction Site:

Measuring Rod: A wooden rod used by carpenters or masons to measure the length, width, and narrowness of bays. It is usually made of one-inch or two-inch foreign pine. Its purpose is to replace the ordinary use of feet, saving time and reducing steps.

Sill Plate (Wooden Plate): Under the position where joists and load-bearing structures are placed, a sill plate must first be laid. Its function is to distribute the pressure of the weight evenly.

Flashing (Flashing): At the gable edges or sloping valleys of tiled roofs, lead sheets are wrapped around the wall or wooden strips. This is called flashing. It can be either step flashing or groove flashing.

Downspout (Water Pipe): A lead or wrought iron pipe next to the eaves, used to direct water to the gutters.

Leader Head (Lead Head): A type of water box that prevents rainwater from rushing down from the roof and directly into the pipes, allowing it to fill the gutter and flow out. (Water Box)

Surface Drain (Surface Drain): Also called an open ditch. A water channel exposed on the ground that directs water into the gutters.

Drain Pipe (Drain Pipe): Also called a culvert. An underground gutter; a pipe for draining water.

Gully (Gully): A type of buffer facility between the surface drain and the drain pipe, similar to the leader head between the gutter and the downspout.

Main Hole (Main Hole): A kind of buffering equipment, it is the prevention method of stopping the excessive water volume of the drain pipes suddenly.

Plumb Board (Plumb Board): Shaped like a pointed arrow, with a recessed notch at the tail for hanging a plumb line. Used to correct the "bulge" or "avoidance" of the wall.

Level Box (Level Box): A simple, crude measuring device made of a whole piece of wood with a hollowed-out center. Water is poured into the hollow, and three T-shaped wooden boards are placed upside down on the water surface. By looking at the straight line at the top of the three wooden boards, one can measure distant targets.

Shenbao Local Supplement: Film Supplement

A Brief History of the Development of Cinema (8) 207

— Wenying

(8) The Story of the First Few Movie Stars

In the previous section, I talked about the original meaning of "Hollywood" and how an unemployed set designer, Robert Blounton, discovered Hollywood. By 1916, Hollywood had become the center of the film world. Except for a few insignificant small companies that continued to work in various places for various reasons, all the important large companies had gathered in Hollywood. After a few more years, the eyes of the world were focused on the surroundings of that wasteland discovered by Robert Blounton.

We have also said before that in the early days of the invention of film, people in the theater industry looked down on movie actors. Famous actors on the stage would never go to film companies to make movies, and smaller actors, in order to earn some extra money, would agree to film secretly, fearing that their peers would know and ridicule them. However, when film companies from all over the world gathered in one place in Hollywood, and the potential of the film industry was unleashed in terms of both talent and financial resources, people in the theater industry could no longer ignore it forever.

The remuneration obtained by movie stars gradually exceeded what stage actors could earn, but Mary Pickford's mother unintentionally raised the status of movie actors in general. She first advised the filmmakers to suddenly inflate Mary's salary and spread the fact as a promotional material. Of course, Mary Pickford's mother's intention was only to allow her daughter to earn more money, but she did not know that in this way, the trend of movie actors earning high salaries began. From then on, the salary of a movie star was more than that of the head of a country, and the originator of this trend was the veteran movie queen, Mary Pickford. Now let's talk about the stories of some of the earliest movie stars.

Among the female stars of that time, in addition to Mary Pickford and Gloria Swanson, May Allison was also a prominent female star. After she came to Hollywood from Georgia, she suddenly became popular. She was one of the major stars of Metro Pictures, but strangely, her dress and behavior were as simple and innocent as a country girl.

At the same time, a romantic woman came from Russia, Nazimova. Her behavior was the opposite of May Allison's. Nazimova was the originator of what modern female stars call "glamour." These two people had completely different personalities, but they shared fame, and each had their own supporters. From this, it can be seen that Hollywood is a gathering place for various talents with different characteristics, and it is still the same today.

At that time, Nazimova's arrogance was so high that it made people retreat. She chose her own scripts, created her own magnificent sets, and made her own gorgeous and novel costumes. In this way, she added an incredible color and seductiveness to her works. This was something Hollywood had never seen before, and the general audience could not help but be fascinated by it. Nazimova was an extremely intelligent person, and she revealed a limitless future everywhere. Everyone felt that she lived for art, and that she would not experience the suffering of the world. But everyone guessed wrong. Now let's briefly talk about Nazimova's story of unrequited love.

When Nazimova came to Hollywood, she came with Charles Bryant. They lived together, and people always thought they were a couple. But soon this Bryant married another woman, and he and Nazimova were not divorced. Originally, he and Nazimova had never been married. Everyone discussed this matter, but they always thought that Nazimova would not be affected by anything. At this time, Paul Bern (who later committed suicide, Jean Harlow's husband) saw her inner sorrow. She was in New York at the time. She told the waiters in the hotel that she would not see any guests and would not answer any outside calls. Paul wanted to see her, but he couldn't. Later, he bribed the waiters and they let him up.

Paul Bern walked into Nazimova's room and persuaded her, "Hey, you can't be like this. You can't let people know you're sad. Quickly put on your most beautiful evening dress. I'll go out with you and let everyone see. This way, people will admire your courage." Nazimova listened to Paul Bern's words, and indeed, changed her clothes and went out with him. They went to all the major nightclubs in New York all night. Those who saw them were whispering and discussing. This incident was the first time that the private lives of movie stars received public attention. Later, the use of stars' marriages and love affairs as promotional materials also started from Nazimova's time. (To be continued)

Two European Actresses Recently Arrived in Hollywood 208

— Fu

We have heard many rumors that London is about to become the second film capital of the world, competing with and defeating Hollywood, and that Hollywood stars are gradually going to Europe, or being attracted to London. However, here, there are already two actresses who have been recruited by Hollywood from Europe. One is British, and the other is German.

The British actress is Merle Oberon, who co-starred with Douglas Fairbanks in "The Private Life of Don Juan." Since she is called the beauty in "The Private Life of Don Juan," her beauty is self-evident. Merle Oberon is indeed a beauty, and it is said that she was the result of several strict selections by the old Fairbanks.

Since "The Private Life of Don Juan" was filmed, although "The Private Life of Don Juan" itself was not a very successful work, the fame of its female lead, Merle Oberon, was very loud for a time, and Hollywood's 20th Century Fox quickly took the lead and recruited her.

It is said that after Merle Oberon arrived in Hollywood, filmmaker Darryl Zanuck spent a huge sum of $35,000 specifically for her makeover expenses. Among them, $25,000 was for wardrobe expenses, and $10,000 was for makeup expenses. This completely transformed a European beauty into the beauty in Hollywood's ideal.

The German actress came from the London film industry. She once played Catherine the Great in "Catherine the Great," so her name was already famous all over the world. She has now set off for the United States. She will first perform on the New York stage for some time, and then go to Hollywood.

This star is Elisabeth Bergner. It is said that she is as timid as a fawn and as afraid as a goat. When she arrives in the United States, from New York to Hollywood, she will avoid all reporters. Some people may say that she is imitating Garbo, but fearing reporters seems to be her nature. When she was in London, British reporters never got an interview with her. Perhaps the all-pervasive American reporters are more capable than British reporters. But perhaps the tough attitude of American reporters makes her even more afraid and avoids them even more.

Elisabeth Bergner's only protector is her multi-talented husband. When she was in England, she and her husband were inseparable. When she was on the set, her husband was always by her side. It is said that when her husband is not around, she will be lost and at a loss.

From this point of view, Hollywood is still recruiting talents from various foreign countries, and it doesn't seem to be declining. As the saying goes, a centipede does not collapse even in death, not to mention that Hollywood has not yet reached the point of death, so how can we say that it is collapsing?

"The Age of Innocence" Made into a Film 209

— Guocheng

Edith Wharton's literary masterpiece "The Age of Innocence," which shook New York society with its dramatic and moving subject matter not many years ago, has recently been adapted and arranged by the screenwriters of the Electric Hua Film Studio, and thus has been brought to the screen.

In the scenes that have been filmed, it strives to preserve the inherent sad atmosphere and plot of the original work, and tries to shorten many unnecessary components to describe a pure and flawless love that was defeated by customs.

The climax of the story is in explaining the strength shown to the male and female protagonists by the high moral and just concept, which has always forced them to bend to consider the code of "proper and polite actions."

Irene Dunne and John Boles play the leading roles in this film as a pair of Unrequiled Lovers. The performances they give to the audience not only maintain the most moving demeanor and actions based on past experience, but also succeed on top of their co-starring in "Back Street."

The main actors appearing in "The Age of Innocence" also include Julie Haydon and five very famous stars of the New York Stage Association – Lionel Atwill, Helen Westley, Laura Hope Crews, etc.

Ten Thousand People Compete to See Mr. Wang 210

The first product of the New Era Company, "Mr. Wang's Secret," with the protagonists "Mr. Wang" and "Little Chen" still played by Tang Jie and Cao Xuesong, and produced by cartoonist Ye Qianyu himself. Since its premiere at the Jin Cheng Grand Theater, it has been more than a week, but the box office is still very crowded. The film is rich in jokes and has many gimmicks. From the opening to the closing, the theater is filled with laughter. Therefore, those who have seen this film have praised it as an unprecedented work of domestic comedy. It is also heard that the theater originally planned to change the film on Friday, but later continued to show it for several days due to excellent business. Those who have not seen this film, please do not miss it.

The Outer Branch of the Ant-Bee Drama Library is Open for Mailing 211

Since the Ant-Bee Drama Library began its trial operation of local mailing, the number of borrowers has been extremely enthusiastic. In order to meet the requirements of people from outside areas, the outer branch for mailing is also opened on March 1st. Local mailing is actively expanded and continues to recruit new readers. All those who love "emerging drama" can participate. Send a stamped envelope and post one cent to No. 15, Lane 310, New Chongqing Road, Shanghai, and it will be sent. A cost of three cents must be attached when requesting a list of books. It is also heard that the first type of loose-leaf play selection "The Misplayed Drama" (written by Masumi Fujii of Japan), selected and compiled by the compilation department of the library, has begun typesetting and is expected to be printed in March.

"Martyr's Blood" is Banned 212

— Wenru

The new film "The Lives of a Bengal Lancer" recently completed by Paramount Pictures of the United States is one of the giant films selected by the company this year. The content describes the suppression of the British army when the Indian tribes rebelled. It was submitted to the Central Film Inspection Committee in the capital for inspection a month ago. It is recently learned that the Film Inspection Committee believes that the film promotes the imperialist suppression of weak nations, which violates Article 1, Paragraph 5 and Article 8 of the Film Inspection Law, and prohibits it from being shown. According to the meeting rules, the company is instructed to return the film to its country, otherwise it will be confiscated. It is also heard that the notification letter was delivered last week.

Film Novel

Grand Old Girl (9) 213

— Shumin

Suddenly there was the sound of a car outside the door, but she was in deep thought and grief, not paying any attention. The door inside and outside had nothing to do with her. Although she wanted to muster up the courage again, she couldn't lift her head for a moment. At this time, only Bose was staring blankly outside the door, utterly bored. He suddenly noticed the cars that had stopped. Several plainclothes detectives jumped out of the first car. Then a tall man walked out of the largest car and hurried towards the school door. Bose quickly opened the door and unconsciously cried out, "The President!" The man nodded slightly and walked in. The tall man walked slowly through the hallway, stopping from time to time to stroke the tables, as if he was touched by something.

He has now walked into the principal's office and is standing in front of Miss Beers. He recited like a child carrying a textbook, "God bless you, little one. Barefoot, carrying…" Miss Beers slowly raised her head, her tearful eyes blurred and she couldn't see who was standing in front of her, so she followed along like she was teaching a primary school student, "Carrying a reddish face." She then wiped away her tears, looked forward, and suddenly stood up with joy and shouted, "How did you come?" The President said kindly, "I am tired of politics… I feel that there are still many things in the world that I have not learned… There are still many things that you can teach me." As he said this, he walked towards Beers. Beers quickly took a step forward, and they embraced each other. At this time, Beers couldn't help but burst into tears.

Outside, Bose had gone mad and spread the news, and people from all over the city were coming to the school one by one. Jielai and Helunte also received the news and rushed over, but Kelalunsidaideby arrived before them. Jielai strode towards the school gate, walking and wondering, "Really? Is the President here? Why is he here?" Daide said, "If you must know, I telegraphed him." Jielai wanted to go in, but Daide stopped him. He said, "Jielai! You stand here with me and everyone else! You are just a country bumpkin, you haven't seen the world, what's the difference between you and others?" Jielai was furious and wanted to push him away, but he couldn't push him away.

After a while, the door opened and the President came out, with Miss Beers on his arm. Everyone was silent when they saw the President come out. The President then opened his mouth and said, "My friends… my fellow villagers… I have nothing to say now. I have come here to rest and think… and to pray… and to thank this good woman who has served society all her life, educated children, and created healthy citizens." He then turned to Miss Beers and said, "I owe my entire career to you, and I thank you especially." There was a burst of cheers from the crowd. At this time, Jielai whispered to Helunte, "Did you hear that? We can't ignore it. We just have to ask her to come back!" Jili and Sangdi, standing near them, heard what they said, and everyone held hands tightly and smiled at each other.

The President still grabbed Miss Beers's hand and said, "I am honored to shake hands with you, my teacher in childhood. In this way, I represent the people of the whole country to express my gratitude to these silent heroes again and again—because their enthusiasm for protecting the youth of the country is no less than the love of parents for their own children!" There was another burst of cheers from the crowd. At this time, Lulan Beers didn't know if she was in heaven or on earth. But she saw Kelalunsidaide, and Daide smiled at her slightly. She also saw the education inspector Helunte. He was a sycophant, and he hurriedly nodded and smiled at Beers. Her eyes then returned to the President. The President looked down at her, and his eyes revealed infinite respect—a brave warrior—able to survive in despair and turn defeat into victory! (The End)
